+1. Introduction
+
+Yardward Pro is a single, integrated operations platform for trucking and haulage companies. It
+consolidates scheduling, driver workflows, fleet management, work orders, billing, real-time GPS, and
+inter-team communications into one app. Before Yardward Pro, a typical haulage business would juggle:
+
+вЂў Workforce or similar for time tracking and shift scheduling
+вЂў Formstack or paper for driver forms (inspections, work orders, dump logs)
+вЂў Fleetio for vehicle maintenance and history
+вЂў Twilio plus a spreadsheet for dispatch SMS
+вЂў QuickBooks Online for invoicing and payroll
+вЂў Email and group chats for between-role coordination
+
+Yardward Pro absorbs every workflow above into a single application with role-specific views вЂ” admin,
+driver, and mechanic вЂ” backed by a single Supabase database. The external systems that remain
+(Twilio, Geotab, QuickBooks, Fleetio, Resend) are integrated, not replaced. Drivers and mechanics in the
+field still receive Twilio SMS notifications, but the dispatcher composes them from inside Yardward Pro
+and every reply is tracked back into the right conversation thread.
+
+1.1. Architecture at a glance
+
+Yardward Pro is delivered as a Progressive Web App (PWA). That means:
+
+вЂў The app loads from a URL in any modern browser вЂ” no app-store download or approval cycle
+вЂў Drivers and mechanics 'install' it from the URL onto their phone home screen with one tap
+вЂў After install it launches in full-screen, looks and feels native, and updates itself automatically when
+
+    admins push new releases
+вЂў Forms submitted in dead zones (rural quarries, basement loading bays, locker rooms) queue locally
+
+    on the device and sync to the database when the device reconnects
+
+The backend is Supabase (managed PostgreSQL with Row-Level Security, Auth, Realtime, Storage, and
+Edge Functions). Every data access path enforces role-based isolation at the database level вЂ” even if a
+frontend bug tried to leak driver A's time entries to driver B, Postgres itself would refuse to return the
+rows.
+
+1.2. Three role-specific views
+
+Yardward Pro presents a different shell depending on which role the signed-in user has:
+
+Field     Description
+Admin
+          Desktop-first sidebar with 17 management tabs
+Driver    covering schedule, fleet, work orders,
+Mechanic  communications, billing, settings, etc. Used by
+          dispatchers, owners, and office staff.
+          Mobile-first bottom-tab nav with 6 tabs (Home, Jobs,
+          Forms, Tickets, Messages, Profile). Used in the cab and
+          on-site by truck drivers and equipment operators.
+          Desktop or tablet sidebar with 6 workshop-focused
+          tabs (Dashboard, Work orders, Messages, POs,
+          Maintenance logs, Inventory). Used in the shop by
+                                                                  mechanics.
+
+в„№пёЏ NOTE Role assignment is server-controlled. An admin assigns the role when they create a user. A driver can
+never elevate themselves to admin вЂ” even attempts to manipulate the JWT or localStorage are blocked by RLS
+at the database level.
+2. Getting started
+
+2.1. Sign-in walkthrough
+
+Open https://yardward-pro.vercel.app/ (or your custom domain) in Chrome, Safari, Firefox, or Edge. The
+sign-in page renders the same on desktop and mobile.
+
+ Yardward Pro sign-in page. Left: hero panel with brand statistics. Right: sign-in form with role chips, email + password, Forgot?
+                                                                link, and Sign in button.
+
+1. Pick your role from the three chips at the top of the form: Admin, Driver, or Mechanic. This is purely
+    a hint вЂ” your actual permissions come from the database.
+
+2. Enter your work email in the Email field. The form accepts any email format that has the shape
+    user@domain.tld; no real-time validation against the database happens at this step.
+
+3. Enter your password in the Password field. Passwords are masked by default; there is no 'show
+    password' toggle in production to prevent shoulder-surfing.
+
+4. Click Sign in to Yardward Pro. The button shows a spinner while authentication runs against
+    Supabase Auth.
+
+5. On success you are redirected to the role-appropriate landing page: /admin for admins, /driver for
+    drivers, /mechanic for mechanics.
+
+    вљ пёЏ WARNING If you enter the wrong password three times in a row, Supabase Auth applies rate limiting. Wait
+    30 seconds before retrying. After ten consecutive failures, the account is temporarily locked вЂ” contact your
+    admin to unlock via the Supabase dashboard.
+2.2. First-time sign-in
+
+When an admin creates your account, they hand you a one-time temporary password (a 16-character
+random string like 'rKszZ@A4!2uCNYJ5'). You must rotate this on first sign-in for security вЂ” anyone who
+saw the temp password during handoff could theoretically log in as you.
+6. Sign in using the temp password your admin gave you. You land on your role's dashboard.
+7. Immediately go back to /login (sign out from your profile or just navigate).
+8. Click the Forgot? link next to the Password label.
+9. An inline panel expands with an email input. The form pre-fills with the email you just typed; verify
+
+    it's yours.
+10. Click Send link. A confirmation toast appears: 'If <email> has an account, a reset link is on its way.'
+11. Open your email and look for a message from noreply@mail.app.supabase.io (or whatever sender
+
+    you've configured in SMTP).
+12. Click the link in the email. You land on the /reset-password page.
+13. Enter a strong new password (minimum 6 characters вЂ” but we strongly recommend 12+ with a mix
+
+    of uppercase, lowercase, digits, and symbols).
+14. Confirm the password in the second field.
+15. Click Update password. The page redirects to /login after a brief success animation.
+16. Sign in with your new password.
+
+        Forgot? panel expanded. Pre-filled with the email already in the sign-in form. Click Send link to fire the reset email.
+
+2.3. Forgot password recovery (existing users)
+
+If you've forgotten your password, the recovery flow is identical to first-time sign-in:
+17. Go to /login.
+18. Click Forgot?, enter your email, and click Send link.
+19. Check your inbox (and spam folder вЂ” until SMTP is configured, the email comes from Supabase's
+
+    default mailer and is often filtered).
+20. Click the link, set a new password, sign in.
+
+н ЅнІЎ TIP Supabase's default mailer is rate-limited to ~4 reset emails per hour across the entire organization. If
+you don't see the email within 60 seconds, ask your admin to use the Admin в†’ Settings в†’ Users tab to rotate
+your password directly (no email required).
+
+2.4. Installing the mobile PWA
+
+Drivers and mechanics should install Yardward Pro to their phone home screen for the best experience.
+After install:
+
+вЂў The app launches in full-screen, without the browser address bar вЂ” feels like a native app
+вЂў App icon shows your Yardward branding on the home screen
+вЂў Notifications integrate with the device's push notification system
+вЂў Forms persist across launches even if you force-close the browser
+
+iOS Safari (iPhone, iPad)
+21. Open the app URL in Safari (must be Safari вЂ” Chrome on iOS cannot install PWAs).
+22. Tap the Share button at the bottom of the screen (square with up-arrow).
+23. Scroll down in the share sheet and tap 'Add to Home Screen'.
+24. Give the shortcut a name (default: 'Yardward Pro').
+25. Tap Add in the top-right.
+26. Close Safari and tap the new icon on your home screen to launch.
+
+Android Chrome
+27. Open the app URL in Chrome.
+28. Tap the three-dot menu in the top-right.
+29. Tap 'Install app' or 'Add to Home screen' (label depends on Chrome version).
+30. Confirm the install in the dialog.
+31. The app icon appears in your app drawer and on your home screen.
+
+в„№пёЏ NOTE After install, you may be prompted to allow notifications and location access. Allow both вЂ”
+Yardward Pro uses location to capture GPS on form submissions (required for compliance) and notifications for
+job assignments and message alerts.
+
+2.5. Roles & access overview
+
+Each role has a strict permission boundary enforced by Postgres Row-Level Security. The table below
+summarizes what each role can see and do:
+
+Field  Description
+Admin
+       Full read/write across all tables. Can
+       create/edit/delete users, vehicles, clients, jobs, work
+       orders. Can observe all Communications threads. Can
+       approve work orders and POs. Can configure org
+Driver    settings and integrations. There is no higher role вЂ”
+Mechanic  admins are the ultimate authority in the org.
+
+          Read/write only on rows where driver_id = their UUID.
+          Can see only jobs assigned to them, vehicle they're
+          assigned, their own time entries, inspections, work
+          orders, and tickets. Can see clients only through the
+          jobs they're working. Cannot see other drivers' data.
+          Can create Communications threads with mechanics;
+          admins can be tagged.
+
+          Read/write on shared shop resources (inventory,
+          tools, maintenance logs, vehicle inspections) plus their
+          own purchase requests and assigned maintenance
+          work orders. Cannot see driver-private data (time
+          entries, individual driver schedules). Can create
+          Communications threads with drivers.
+3. Admin guide
+
+The admin shell is a left-sidebar layout with 17 navigation tabs. The sidebar is fixed on desktop (width
+240px) and collapses behind a hamburger menu on tablets and below. The top bar shows the current
+page title and a notifications bell that pulses when there's unread activity.
+
+3.1. Dashboard
+
+                                                 Admin dashboard вЂ” landing page after sign-in.
+
+The dashboard is your morning check. It summarizes the operational state of the business at a glance
+and links into every detail screen below.
+Layout
+Three rows of content:
+вЂў KPI strip вЂ” quick numeric summary cards: active drivers, scheduled jobs today, work orders
+
+    awaiting approval, POs pending, overdue maintenance, etc.
+вЂў Today's schedule вЂ” a horizontally-scrollable view of every job scheduled for today, sorted by start
+    time. Click any card to open the job detail sheet.
+
+вЂў Recent activity feed вЂ” last 10 notifications from the notifications table, sorted newest-first. Color
+    dots indicate type: green=positive, amber=pending action, red=alert/flag, blue=informational.
+
+Common workflows from the dashboard
+вЂў Click a KPI card to drill into the relevant tab (e.g. 'Work orders awaiting approval' takes you to
+
+    /admin/work-orders filtered to pending)
+вЂў Click a job card in the schedule strip to review or edit its details
+вЂў Click an activity entry to navigate to the source (notification with a link field)
+
+3.2. Schedule
+
+      Weekly schedule grid. Rows are drivers; columns are weekdays. Cells show assigned job cards or a + quick-add button.
+
+The schedule is the dispatcher's primary workspace. It's a weekly grid showing every driver on the y-axis
+and the 7 days of the current week on the x-axis. Each {driver, day} cell either contains a job card (the
+driver is assigned a job that day) or a faint + button revealed on hover (the cell is empty and you can
+quick-add).
+Creating a new job
+Two paths:
+вЂў Click the 'Create new job' button at the top of the page вЂ” opens an empty dialog
+вЂў Click the + in a specific {driver, weekday} cell вЂ” opens the dialog with that driver and date pre-filled
+Create Job dialog. Fields for client, address, date, time, driver, vehicle, and notes.
+
+Create Job dialog fields                   Description
+
+Field                                      Required. Select from your client roster. The client's
+Client                                     rate table determines what the invoice will look like
+                                           once the work order is approved.
+Address                                    Free-text job site address. Used for SMS dispatch and
+Date                                       the live map. Add a postal code for best results.
+Time                                       Job date in YYYY-MM-DD format. Defaults to today (or
+                                           the weekday you clicked the + cell for).
+Driver                                     Scheduled start time in HH:MM 24-hour format. Used
+Vehicle                                    for sorting in the schedule grid and the driver's Home
+                                           screen.
+Notes                                      Required. Pick from active drivers. Pre-filled if you
+                                           opened the dialog from a specific row.
+Save as Draft vs. Publish & notify driver  Required. Pre-fills with the driver's currently assigned
+The dialog has two submit actions:         vehicle, but you can override (e.g. for swap-truck
+                                           days).
+                                           Optional free-text. Internal dispatcher notes вЂ”
+                                           appended to the SMS sent to the driver when you
+                                           publish.
+
+вЂў Save as draft вЂ” the job is created with status='draft'. Drafts are private to admins; the driver does
+    not see them and no SMS is sent. Use this when finalizing details over several edits.
+вЂў Publish + notify driver вЂ” the job goes live (status='published'), shows up in the driver's My Jobs and
+    Today's schedule, and a Twilio SMS is dispatched immediately with the job summary, time, address,
+    and any notes.
+
+    вљ пёЏ WARNING Once a job is published, you can edit it but the driver does NOT get a second SMS. Material
+    changes (different time, different address) should be communicated separately via the Communications tab or
+    by phone.
+
+Editing or rescheduling
+32. Click any existing job card in the grid.
+33. The Edit Job sheet opens on the right with the same fields as Create Job, plus a Status dropdown
+
+    (Draft / Published / In progress / Completed / Delayed / Cancelled).
+34. Make changes; click Save changes.
+35. If you change the driver or date, the card moves in the grid automatically (realtime via Supabase
+
+    Realtime subscriptions).
+
+3.3. Jobs
+
+                                           All jobs across all dates, with status filter pills and search.
+
+The Jobs tab is the flat list view of every job вЂ” past, present, and future. Use it when you need to find a
+specific job or look back at history.
+Filtering
+вЂў Search box вЂ” matches client name, address, driver name, and job ID (substring, case-insensitive)
+вЂў Status pills вЂ” All / Pending / In Progress / Completed. Click to filter; click again to clear
+вЂў Date range picker (when expanded) вЂ” narrow to a billing period or week
+Per-row actions
+Click any row to open the side-sheet with the job's full lifecycle:
+вЂў Job details (client, address, scheduled time, vehicle, driver, notes)
+вЂў Status transitions log (when the job moved Draft в†’ Published в†’ In progress в†’ Completed)
+вЂў Linked work order if the driver has submitted one
+вЂў Linked invoice if the work order has been approved
+вЂў GPS map showing the job site and any clock-in/clock-out points from the driver
+вЂў Communications threads tagged to this job (filtered by topic_ref_id=job.id)
+
+3.4. Drivers & mechanics
+
+Drivers + mechanics roster. Each card shows avatar, name, status badge, phone, license info. Pencil icon opens phone-edit sheet.
+
+This is your staff roster. Both drivers and mechanics live in this tab, displayed in two sections.
+The yellow phone-placeholder warning
+If any driver or mechanic has a phone number that isn't a valid E.164 (e.g. they have a US format like
+'555-123-4567' or a blank field), a yellow banner at the top of the page counts them. Twilio outbound
+SMS will NOT deliver to placeholder numbers вЂ” job assignments and Communications messages get
+silently dropped for those people.
+36. Click the pencil icon on a card with a placeholder phone.
+37. A sheet opens with the current phone and a new-phone input.
+38. Enter the real number in E.164 format: + then country code then number, no spaces (e.g.
+
+    +14165550100 for a Toronto landline).
+39. The Save button only enables when the format is valid AND the new value differs from the current.
+40. Click Save phone. The card updates immediately; the next SMS to that person will deliver.
+Adding a new driver
+
+Add Driver dialog. Name, email, E.164 phone, license number, license expiry. The Phone field placeholder is the recommended
+                                                                        format.
+
+Click 'Add driver' at the top-right of the roster.
+
+Field                                               Description
+Name
+Email                                               Required. Full name; first name shows in greeting
+Phone (E.164)                                       cards, full name shows in lookups and invoices.
+                                                    Required, must be a deliverable address. The driver
+License number                                      will sign in with this email. Cannot be changed later
+License expiry                                      without admin intervention.
+                                                    Optional but strongly recommended вЂ” without it, the
+On click 'Add driver', Yardward Pro:                driver cannot receive job-assignment SMS or
+                                                    Communications messages on their phone. Format:
+                                                    +<country><number> with no spaces or punctuation.
+                                                    Required for drivers. Will be displayed on the driver's
+                                                    profile card and used for compliance reporting. Free-
+                                                    text вЂ” accepts any format your jurisdiction uses.
+                                                    Required for drivers. YYYY-MM-DD. Yardward Pro can
+                                                    be configured to warn the driver and admin N days
+                                                    before expiry.
+
+41. Validates the inputs (email format, phone E.164 if provided, license expiry is a real date)
+42. Calls the admin-create-user edge function which uses the Supabase Auth Admin API to create the
+
+    auth user with a random 16-character temporary password
+43. Inserts a row into the profiles table with the email, name, and role='driver' via the
+    handle_new_auth_user trigger
+
+44. Patches the phone field onto the new profile
+45. Inserts a row into the drivers side table with license_number, license_expiry, and computed initials
+46. Shows you a 'Driver created' panel with the email, the temp password, and a Copy credentials
+
+    button
+
+    н ЅнІЎ TIP Click Copy credentials to put 'Email: <email>\nTemp password: <pw>' on the clipboard. Paste into a
+    Slack DM, SMS, or email to hand off to the new driver. They use the credentials to sign in once, then
+    immediately rotate via Forgot? as described in section 2.2.
+
+3.5. Vehicles
+
+   Fleet roster. Each card shows vehicle ID, year, type (truck/trailer/equipment), assigned driver, odometer, engine hours, last
+                                                      service date, and next service due date.
+
+Yardward Pro tracks every vehicle in your fleet вЂ” trucks, trailers, equipment, anything you want
+maintenance tracking on. Each vehicle has:
+вЂў A unique ID (e.g. TRK-07, EQ-02) вЂ” used everywhere as the human-readable identifier
+вЂў Full make/model/year metadata
+вЂў An assigned primary driver (optional; one driver per vehicle at a time)
+вЂў Odometer and engine hours, kept in sync with Geotab telemetry
+вЂў Last service date and next service due date
+вЂў Status: operational, in maintenance, or out of service
+Adding a vehicle
+Click 'Add vehicle' at the top. The dialog accepts ID (auto-generated suggestion T-NN), name, year, type,
+current odometer, engine hours, and Geotab device ID if you have one to wire up GPS tracking.
+
+Importing from Fleetio
+If you're migrating off Fleetio, click 'Import from Fleetio'. The import edge function reads from your
+Fleetio account (via the FLEETIO_BEARER_TOKEN secret) and brings in:
+
+вЂў Every vehicle with full metadata
+вЂў Maintenance history (every service event with parts, labor, cost)
+вЂў Fuel logs
+
+Use 'Dry run' mode first to see what would be imported without writing anything. Then disable dry-run
+and click Run import вЂ” typically takes 30-60 seconds for a 50-vehicle fleet.
+
+Vehicle detail page
+Click any vehicle card to open its detail page. Tabs:
+
+вЂў Overview вЂ” current status, assigned driver, embedded GPS map showing where the vehicle is
+    RIGHT NOW
+
+вЂў Maintenance вЂ” chronological log of every service event, including ones logged from the mechanic
+    shop
+
+вЂў Fuel вЂ” fill-up log with mpg/L per 100km calculations
+вЂў Tools вЂ” assigned tools (from the tool checklist module)
+вЂў History вЂ” timeline of status changes
+3.6. Live vehicle map
+
+  Live map of every vehicle in the fleet, pulled from Geotab. Color-coded markers by status. Sidebar lists vehicles with last-seen
+                                                                           times.
+
+The live map shows every vehicle's current location, updated every 30 seconds. Markers are color-
+coded:
+вЂў Green вЂ” operational and on schedule
+вЂў Amber вЂ” in maintenance (currently in the shop)
+вЂў Gray вЂ” out of service
+вЂў Red вЂ” alert (e.g. prolonged stop detected, exceeded route boundary)
+How the map gets data
+Yardward Pro polls Geotab's API every 5 minutes via a Supabase cron job (the geotab-sync-locations
+edge function). The poll fetches each vehicle's last known coordinates, last heading, last odometer
+reading, and engine hours, and writes them into the vehicle_locations table. The map subscribes to that
+table via Supabase Realtime вЂ” so changes show up on your screen within a second of Geotab returning
+new data.
+Common workflows
+вЂў Click a marker вЂ” opens a popup with vehicle ID, driver name, last-seen time, and 'Open detail'
+
+    deep-link
+вЂў Click a sidebar row вЂ” recenters the map and zooms to that vehicle
+вЂў Use the search box (top of sidebar) вЂ” find by vehicle ID or driver name
+вЂў 'Refresh now' button (top-right) вЂ” forces an immediate Geotab poll instead of waiting for the cron
+3.7. Work orders
+
+   Submitted work orders awaiting management review. Columns: WO ID, job, driver, client, weight tonnes, dump site, status,
+                                                                     submitted time.
+
+A work order is the driver's record of work performed at a job site вЂ” load type, weight, dump location,
+foreman signature, and any photos. When a driver completes a job, they submit a work order from their
+mobile app; it lands here for management review.
+The approval flow
+47. Driver submits the work order from /driver/work-order. The submission includes GPS check-in
+
+    (where the WO was submitted), foreman signature drawn on touchscreen, weight in tonnes, dump
+    site, and any photos.
+48. The WO arrives here with status='pending'. The admin gets a notification.
+49. Click the WO row to open the review sheet. You can see every field, the captured signature, GPS
+    map, and photos.
+50. Click Approve to authorize invoicing. Yardward Pro auto-generates the QuickBooks invoice draft
+    using the client's rate table вЂ” the line items are looked up based on the work order's load type and
+    weight. The invoice draft lands in the Forms & Submissions в†’ Invoices tab where you can review
+    before pushing to QBO.
+51. OR click Reject. A dialog asks for a rejection reason (free-text, required). The driver gets a
+    notification with the reason and can resubmit a corrected work order.
+
+    в„№пёЏ NOTE Only one approval action is allowed per work order вЂ” the approve_work_order Supabase RPC uses
+    a row-level FOR UPDATE lock to prevent two admins from approving the same WO twice and creating duplicate
+    invoices.
+3.8. Communications
+
+Communications inbox. Left rail: thread list with filter chips (Tagged me / Joined / All). Right pane: selected thread with
+                                                       messages and compose box.
+
+Communications is Yardward Pro's central messaging surface. It implements a customer-specific
+topology: driverв†”mechanic threads are the primary channel; admin has read-everything visibility for
+oversight, but doesn't get notifications by default. Admins become active participants only when
+explicitly tagged by a driver or mechanic, or when they self-join a thread to intervene.
+
+Filter chips         Description
+
+Field                DEFAULT. Shows only threads where the admin is an
+Tagged me            active participant. This is the admin's 'inbox' вЂ”
+                     threads requiring their attention.
+Joined               Threads where the admin has self-joined to observe or
+All                  intervene, but wasn't formally tagged.
+                     Every conversation in the org вЂ” RLS allows admin to
+                     read all threads even when not participating. Use to
+                     monitor general activity.
+Starting a new conversation
+
+           New Conversation dialog (admin path). Topic, subject, participant checkboxes for both drivers and mechanics.
+
+52. Click 'New' at the top-right of the thread list.
+53. Pick a topic from the dropdown: general, job, vehicle, or maintenance.
+54. Enter a subject (one-line summary of what the thread is about).
+55. Check participants from the drivers + mechanics list. You can include multiple вЂ” useful for cross-role
+
+    coordination.
+56. Click 'Open conversation'. The thread is created, you're added as originator, and the right pane
+
+    switches to the new thread.
+Inside a thread
+The thread view shows:
+вЂў Participant pills at the top вЂ” initials + role badge for each active member; admins joined-not-tagged
+
+    show '(observing)' suffix until they post
+вЂў Message list вЂ” scrolls oldest-to-newest, with your messages right-aligned and others' left-aligned
+вЂў Compose box at the bottom with paperclip (attach photo or PDF), @ button (tag admin вЂ”
+
+    drivers/mechanics only), and send button
+вЂў Close button (admin or originator only) вЂ” archives the thread with optional resolution notes
+
+    н ЅнІЎ TIP If you're observing a thread (filter = All) and need to intervene, you'll see a 'Join conversation' button
+    instead of the compose box. Click Join, then you become a participant and can post + receive notifications.
+3.9. Timesheets
+
+             Weekly timesheet view with clock-in/clock-out events cross-referenced against Geotab vehicle movement.
+
+Timesheets show every driver's clock-in/clock-out events for the selected week, with automatic cross-
+reference against Geotab telemetry.
+How GPS cross-reference works
+When a driver clocks in, Yardward Pro records their GPS location (captured by the device). It then asks
+Geotab where the assigned vehicle was at that exact moment. If the two coordinates are within the GPS
+tolerance (configurable in Settings в†’ System, default 15 minutes / 200 meters), the entry is OK. If not,
+the row is flagged.
+Flag reasons
+вЂў GPS mismatch вЂ” driver clocked in from a different location than the truck was
+вЂў Truck never moved вЂ” driver clocked in but the vehicle stayed stationary for the entire shift (possible
+
+    time-card fraud)
+вЂў Prolonged stop вЂ” the vehicle stopped for >2 hours mid-shift without a corresponding job site visit
+вЂў Overtime threshold вЂ” driver exceeded the configured warning or alert hour threshold
+Export to QuickBooks
+Click 'Export to QuickBooks' at the top-right. The qbo-push-time edge function batches every approved
+time entry for the week into QBO TimeActivity records using the configured QBO_REALM_ID. Each
+driver must have a corresponding QBO Employee mapping configured (Settings в†’ Integrations в†’ QBO
+mappings).
+    вљ пёЏ WARNING Once you've pushed time entries to QBO, you cannot edit them in Yardward Pro вЂ” the
+    qbo_payroll_pushes table records which entries were pushed and prevents re-export. If you need to correct a
+    pushed entry, void it in QBO directly.
+
+3.10. SMS log
+
+           Every Twilio SMS dispatched with delivery status.
+
+The SMS log is the audit trail for every Twilio SMS Yardward Pro has sent.
+
+Field      Description
+Sent at
+           ISO timestamp of when the SMS was queued with
+Driver     Twilio. The actual delivery happens within seconds but
+Job        can be delayed by carrier.
+Message    Recipient вЂ” looked up from drivers.id
+Twilio ID  Linked job (if the SMS was a job assignment
+Delivery   notification).
+           Body of the SMS. Truncated in the table; click row to
+           see full.
+           Twilio's message SID (SM...). Useful when contacting
+           Twilio support.
+           Current delivery status: queued, sent, delivered,
+           failed. Updated in real-time via Twilio delivery
+           webhooks (when configured).
+
+н ЅнІЎ TIP If a driver claims they never received a job assignment, look here first. A 'failed' status with error code
+30003 means the driver's phone is unreachable (powered off, no service). 30007 means the message was
+blocked as spam by the carrier вЂ” common with stock Twilio phone numbers; consider a registered short code
+for high-volume sends.
+3.11. Purchase orders
+
+                                        PO requests from mechanics awaiting management approval.
+
+When a mechanic needs a part for a maintenance work order, they submit a PO request from
+/mechanic. The PO lands here.
+The inventory check
+When a mechanic types a part name in the PO form, Yardward Pro queries the parts inventory in real-
+time and shows matching items inline. If the part is already in stock with sufficient quantity, the
+mechanic is encouraged to pull from inventory rather than submit a PO. This prevents over-ordering.
+If the part isn't in stock or the mechanic submits anyway, the request lands here with an inventory
+snapshot вЂ” admin can see whether the suggestion-to-pull-from-stock was offered to the mechanic and
+overridden.
+PO statuses
+вЂў pending вЂ” submitted by mechanic, awaiting admin review
+вЂў approved вЂ” admin authorized the purchase; mechanic can order
+вЂў ordered вЂ” admin marked as ordered (typically after they've placed the order with the supplier)
+вЂў received вЂ” admin marked as received (parts arrived); the qty_on_hand is bumped via the inventory
+
+    adjustment
+вЂў rejected вЂ” admin denied with a reason
+Approving a PO
+Click the PO row to review. The sheet shows the part name, requested qty, cost estimate, the mechanic
+who submitted, and the maintenance work order it's tied to (if any).
+57. If you want to approve, click Approve. The PO status becomes 'approved' and the mechanic is
+    notified.
+
+58. If you've already placed the order with the supplier, click 'Mark ordered'. The PO becomes 'ordered'.
+59. When parts arrive, open the PO again and click 'Mark received'. Yardward Pro adjusts the inventory
+
+    qty_on_hand automatically.
+60. OR click Reject. A reason dialog appears. The mechanic gets a notification with the reason; they can
+
+    resubmit if appropriate.
+
+3.12. Prepaid tickets
+
+              Per-client prepaid ticket balances.
+
+Prepaid tickets is a billing model used in waste hauling and similar industries: a client buys tickets in bulk
+(e.g. 100 tickets at a flat per-ticket rate), and the driver pulls one ticket per load. The Prepaid Tickets tab
+shows every client's current balance.
+
+Field         Description
+Client
+Balance       Linked client.
+              Current ticket count. Decrements when drivers record
+Threshold     ticket pulls in /driver/tickets.
+              Low-balance trigger. When the balance hits this value,
+Bundle size   Yardward Pro notifies admin to start a replenishment.
+              How many tickets are in one purchase bundle (typical:
+Bundle price  50 or 100).
+              Price per bundle. Used to auto-generate the
+Auto-billing  replenishment invoice.
+              Boolean. If on, Yardward Pro generates the
+              replenishment invoice automatically when the
+              threshold is hit. If off, admin manually triggers.
+Report frequency  How often the client receives a usage report email: off
+                  / daily / weekly / monthly.
+3.13. Clients
+
+                                                  Client roster with contact info and rate tables.
+
+The clients tab is your customer roster. Each client has a contact (name + email + phone), a billing
+address, an optional rate table that drives invoice line items, and optional prepaid ticket settings.
+Creating a new client
+
+                        New Client dialog. Company name, primary contact, email, phone, billing address, notes.
+
+61. Click 'New client' at the top-right.
+62. Fill in Company name (required), Primary contact name, Email (optional but recommended for
+
+    invoice delivery), Phone, Billing address, Notes.
+63. Click Create client. The client is added to the roster; you can now schedule jobs against them.
+Rate tables
+Click a client row to open their detail sheet. The Rate table section lets you define custom pricing per
+load type or vehicle type:
+вЂў Each line item specifies: load type (e.g. 'Topsoil', 'Recycled concrete', 'General waste'), vehicle type
+
+    (truck/trailer/equipment), unit (per tonne / per load / per hour), and unit price
+вЂў When a work order is approved against this client, Yardward Pro looks up the matching line item
+
+    and generates the QBO invoice with the right qty * unit price
+вЂў Falls back through the unit chain: per-tonne match first, then per-load, then per-hour
+3.14. Forms & submissions
+
+                                                Centralized inbox for every form a driver submits.
+
+Forms & Submissions is the central inbox for everything drivers fill out on the mobile app. The page has
+tab pills filtering by form type:
+вЂў Inspections вЂ” vehicle pre-trip and end-of-trip safety inspections
+вЂў Tool checklists вЂ” start and end of shift tool inventory
+вЂў Work orders вЂ” on-site work-order submissions awaiting management review
+вЂў Start of day вЂ” clock-in events with GPS
+вЂў End of day вЂ” clock-out events
+вЂў Job logs вЂ” free-form notes during a job
+вЂў Ticket photos вЂ” driver-uploaded photos of paper tickets pulled for prepaid clients
+Each submission row shows: driver, vehicle (where applicable), submitted timestamp, GPS coordinates if
+captured (clickable, opens a map), and a Resolve button if the submission is informational. Click any row
+to open the full detail sheet with all answers, photos, signature (if collected), and the GPS map.
+3.15. Tenders
+
+                                            Aggregated tender feed scraped from municipal portals.
+
+The Tenders tab is an aggregated feed of contract opportunities scraped from configured municipal
+portals. By default Yardward Pro is configured for Halton region (Ontario), but you can add additional
+sources via the tender_sources table.
+How the scraper runs
+A Supabase cron job runs the tender-scrape edge function every Monday at 06:00 UTC. The function
+loops over enabled tender_sources, scrapes each portal's tender listings, and inserts new rows into the
+tenders table.
+Weekly digest email
+After scraping, the function compiles a digest email summarizing new tenders from the past week and
+sends it to TENDER_DIGEST_RECIPIENTS via Resend. The email is plain text with title, source, deadline,
+and link to the original tender. Configure recipients in Settings в†’ Integrations в†’ Tender digest.
+
+    в„№пёЏ NOTE If RESEND_API_KEY is not configured, the scraper still runs but skips the email send with a warning
+    logged to error_log.
+
+On-demand controls
+вЂў 'Run scraper now' вЂ” fires the scrape function immediately. Useful when you've just added a new
+
+    source or want to refresh outside the weekly cadence.
+вЂў 'Send test digest' вЂ” composes and sends the digest email to the configured recipients on demand.
+
+    Useful for verifying SMTP setup.
+3.16. Error log
+
+                  Error log with severity, source, code, message, and resolve action. Includes Dead-letter queue tab.
+
+The error log captures every notable failure across the app:
+вЂў React error boundaries вЂ” uncaught exceptions in the frontend
+вЂў Edge Function failures вЂ” webhook signature mismatches, Twilio errors, QBO push errors
+вЂў RPC errors вЂ” Supabase SECURITY DEFINER function exceptions
+вЂў Webhook handler errors вЂ” anything that fell into the catch-all outer try
+вЂў Inbound SMS that couldn't be routed (no matching profile by phone)
+Each row has a severity (info / warning / error / critical), source, error code (machine-readable),
+message (human-readable), context (JSON blob with relevant IDs), stack trace (for code errors), and the
+user who triggered it.
+Resolving errors
+Click any row to open the detail sheet. The Resolve action marks the error as resolved with optional
+notes. Resolved errors filter out of the main view (toggleable). Use the Severity filter to focus on
+critical/error rows first.
+Dead-letter queue
+The Dead-letter queue tab shows form submissions that exhausted their retry budget. When a driver
+submits a form offline and the device retries the sync over and over without success, eventually the
+submission lands here. Click 'Requeue' to attempt one more sync; if the underlying issue (e.g. RLS
+violation, malformed data) isn't fixed it will fail again.
+3.17. Reports
+
+                                            Operational reports menu вЂ” cards for each report type.
+
+Yardward Pro includes operational reports for management decision-making:
+вЂў Hours summary вЂ” weekly/monthly driver hours, with flagged events broken out
+вЂў Vehicle utilization вЂ” % time operational vs. in maintenance vs. out of service
+вЂў Revenue by client вЂ” invoice totals per client over selected period
+вЂў Flagged events вЂ” every flag of any kind (GPS mismatches, tool damage, overtime warnings)
+вЂў Maintenance costs вЂ” total $ spent on parts and labor per vehicle
+вЂў Tender pipeline вЂ” submitted bids and win/loss outcomes
+Click any report card to open. Each report has a date-range picker, optional filters (client, driver,
+vehicle), and a chart + data table. Click 'Export PDF' or 'Export CSV' to download for sharing or further
+analysis.
+
+3.18. Settings
+
+The Settings tab has six sub-tabs covering all org-level configuration.
+Organization profile
+
+                                  Organization tab вЂ” business name, tax ID, address, timezone, currency.
+
+These fields render across the app: header brand, invoice header, timezone-aware date displays,
+currency symbol on financial reports. Set them once during onboarding and update only when business
+details change. Click 'Save changes' вЂ” the values persist to the app_settings singleton row in Supabase.
+System thresholds
+
+System tab вЂ” GPS tolerance, overtime warning/alert hours, inspection min/max duration.
+
+Field                              Description
+GPS tolerance (minutes)
+                                   How wide a window Yardward Pro accepts between
+Overtime warning (hours)           driver's clock-in GPS and the vehicle's GPS at the same
+Overtime alert (hours)             moment. Default 15. Lower = stricter.
+Inspection min duration (seconds)  Driver hours threshold at which a warning notification
+Inspection max duration (seconds)  fires. Default 40.
+                                   Driver hours threshold at which a critical alert fires.
+                                   Default 44. Must be greater than warning.
+                                   Minimum time a pre-trip inspection should take.
+                                   Faster than this = likely rushed. Default 780 (13 min).
+                                   Maximum reasonable inspection time. Slower = likely
+                                   distracted. Default 1200 (20 min).
+Integrations
+
+                                 Integrations tab вЂ” Twilio, Geotab, QBO, Fleetio, Resend connection cards.
+
+Each integration has a connection card showing current status (connected / not connected / error) and
+Test / Connect / Disconnect buttons. Configuration values come from Supabase function secrets (set via
+supabase secrets set), not from this UI вЂ” these cards only show status and let you trigger health checks.
+Users
+
+                                Users tab вЂ” roster of all admins, mechanics, drivers with Invite user button.
+
+The Users tab lists every active user in the org and lets admins invite new ones. Click 'Invite user' to open
+a dialog with email, name, optional phone, role selector (admin/driver/mechanic), and conditional
+fields. If role=driver, two extra fields appear: license number and license expiry. On submit, Yardward
+Pro creates the auth user via the admin-create-user edge function and shows you the credentials panel
+for handoff.
+Notifications
+
+                                  Notifications tab вЂ” org-wide toggle switches for each notification type.
+
+Org-wide defaults for notification types: new job assigned SMS, work order awaiting approval, tool
+flagged on checklist, GPS mismatch on time entry, PO awaiting approval, vehicle maintenance overdue,
+daily summary email. Drivers and mechanics can override these per-user via their profile.
+Billing
+
+                 Billing tab вЂ” subscription plan, renewal date, seats used, vehicles active, Cancel subscription button.
+
+Shows your current subscription state. Plan name, renewal date, seats used vs. limit, active vehicles vs.
+limit. The 'Cancel subscription' button opens a confirm dialog with an optional reason; on submit it flips
+billing_status to 'cancel-requested' and notifies the Yardward team. Your subscription remains active
+until the next renewal date; you'll receive a follow-up to confirm.
+4. Driver guide (mobile)
+
+The driver shell is mobile-first. The bottom navigation bar has 6 tabs and stays visible at all times. Forms
+are designed for one-handed use with large tap targets вЂ” drivers wearing gloves or working in poor light
+can still hit the right buttons.
+4.1. Home
+
+                       Driver home screen вЂ” today's jobs, clock-in button, GPS status badge, quick links to forms.
+
+The home screen is your morning check. It shows:
+вЂў GPS status badge at the top вЂ” green if active and accurate, amber if in fallback mode (using last
+    known position), gray if pending
+
+вЂў Clock-in / Clock-out button вЂ” big touch target. Tap to start your shift
+вЂў Pre-trip inspection lockout indicator вЂ” if you haven't done your pre-trip in the last 12 hours, you
+
+    can't clock in (CVOR rule)
+вЂў Today's jobs list вЂ” each card shows scheduled time, client, address, truck
+вЂў Quick links вЂ” shortcuts to Start of day, Tool checklist, Inspection, Work order
+4.2. My jobs
+
+                                   Today's and upcoming jobs assigned to you, sorted by scheduled time.
+
+The Jobs tab shows your full schedule. Today's jobs are highlighted at the top; future jobs are below. Tap
+any job to open its details:
+вЂў Client name and full address (tappable вЂ” opens in your phone's map app for directions)
+вЂў Scheduled start time
+вЂў Assigned vehicle
+вЂў Dispatcher notes (anything the admin added during scheduling)
+вЂў Submit work order button вЂ” opens /driver/work-order with the job context pre-filled
+4.3. Forms tile menu
+
+                                               Forms tile menu вЂ” large tiles for each driver form.
+The Forms tab is a tile menu вЂ” large tappable tiles for each form. From here you can jump into any of
+the driver workflows below.
+
+4.4. Start of day & clock-in
+
+                                     Start of day form вЂ” vehicle selection, GPS captured, optional notes.
+
+Start of day clocks you in for the shift.
+64. Tap Forms в†’ Start of day (or tap the big Clock-in button on Home).
+65. Confirm the vehicle you're driving (pre-selected if you have an assigned truck, but overridable).
+66. Wait for the GPS badge to turn green вЂ” this captures your current location for cross-reference
+
+    against Geotab telemetry.
+67. Optional: add a note (e.g. 'Late start due to weather').
+68. Tap Submit. The form is saved; you're clocked in.
+
+    вљ пёЏ WARNING If you haven't completed a passing pre-trip inspection in the last 12 hours, the Submit button is
+    disabled with a banner: 'Complete inspection first'. Tap the banner to jump to /driver/inspection.
+4.5. Tool checklist
+                                      Tool checklist вЂ” per-vehicle tool inventory with OK / Flag toggles.
+
+The tool checklist verifies your truck's tool inventory at start and end of shift. Each tool has three
+possible states:
+
+вЂў OK (default) вЂ” tool is present and in working condition
+вЂў Missing вЂ” tool is not in the truck
+вЂў Damaged вЂ” tool is present but broken
+
+Any item flagged Missing or Damaged requires a note explaining the issue. Yardward Pro notifies admin
+and the assigned mechanic immediately so they can dispatch a replacement or schedule a repair.
+
+    н ЅнІЎ TIP You can't complete End of day without a passing end-of-shift tool checklist. Get into the habit of
+    running the checklist at the start of every shift (so any missing tool can be addressed before you leave the yard)
+    and again before you submit End of day.
+4.6. Vehicle inspection (pre-trip)
+                          Pre-trip safety inspection вЂ” tyres, lights, brakes, etc. Photo capture for flagged items.
+
+The pre-trip inspection is required by CVOR (Commercial Vehicle Operator's Registration) before every
+shift. Yardward Pro guides you through 8 inspection categories with a checklist of items per category.
+
+Inspection categories
+вЂў Tyres & wheels вЂ” tread depth, sidewall damage, lug nuts
+вЂў Lights & indicators вЂ” headlights, brake lights, signals, hazards
+вЂў Brakes вЂ” feel of pedal, parking brake, air pressure if applicable
+вЂў Fluid levels вЂ” engine oil, coolant, brake fluid, transmission, washer fluid
+вЂў Signage & decals вЂ” DOT numbers, CVOR sticker, hazard signs
+вЂў Coupling devices (if towing) вЂ” kingpin, fifth wheel, safety chains
+вЂў Mirrors & windows вЂ” cracks, visibility, wiper function
+вЂў Cab equipment вЂ” seatbelts, fire extinguisher, first aid kit
+
+Submitting the inspection
+69. Walk around the truck doing the physical inspection.
+70. In the app, tap each item to mark it OK or flag it with a defect category.
+71. Flagged items require: a note describing the issue AND a photo (auto-attached from the camera).
+72. The form saves drafts every 5 seconds вЂ” if you lose signal mid-form, your progress is preserved.
+73. When all items are checked, tap Submit. The form captures: timestamp, GPS, inspection duration,
+
+    vehicle, all answers, all photos.
+
+    в„№пёЏ NOTE A passing inspection unlocks the 12-hour drive window. The system tracks last_pretrip_at on the
+    vehicle. If you try to clock in or submit a work order more than 12 hours after the last passing pretrip, you're
+    locked out until you redo the inspection.
+
+    вљ пёЏ WARNING If you flag any item as Critical (brakes, tyres, fluid leaks), the inspection is failed and the vehicle
+    is auto-flagged out_of_service. Admin and mechanic are notified immediately. Do NOT drive a failed-inspection
+    vehicle.
+4.7. Job log
+
+                                      Job log вЂ” free-form notes during a shift. Anchored to current job.
+
+The job log is your dictation surface. Use it to record anything noteworthy during the shift вЂ” delay
+reasons, client disputes, equipment issues, conversations with customers. Each entry is timestamped +
+GPS-tagged automatically.
+Use the job log entries later when:
+вЂў Disputing a customer complaint ('I told them at 10:23 AM that we needed access to the back lot')
+вЂў Explaining to admin why a job took longer than estimated
+вЂў Documenting an incident for compliance records
+вЂў Tracking patterns (e.g. a recurring issue with a specific client)
+4.8. Work order submission
+Work order form вЂ” load type, weight, dump site, foreman signature, photos, GPS check-in.
+
+The work order is the most important form in the driver workflow. Submit one per completed delivery.
+After admin approval, the invoice auto-generates and bills the client.
+
+Work order fields  Description
+
+Field              Required. Select the job this work order is for. Pre-
+Job                filled if you came from /driver/jobs.
+Load type          Required. Picker вЂ” list of load types is configured per-
+Weight (tonnes)    client in their rate table.
+                   Required. Manual entry. Decimal allowed (e.g. 12.4).
+Dump site          In a future release, will integrate with scale-house
+Work performed     ticket photos.
+Foreman signature  Required. Auto-populated from job location but
+Photo              editable.
+GPS check-in       Free-text description of the work.
+                   Required. The on-site foreman signs the touchscreen.
+                   Stored as a PNG.
+                   Optional but recommended. A photo of the delivered
+                   load or the dump site. Multiple allowed.
+                   Automatic. Captures the GPS coordinates where the
+                   form was submitted. Used for cross-reference if the
+                   work order is disputed.
+
+After submission
+74. The work order lands in admin's Work Orders tab with status='pending'.
+75. Admin reviews and clicks Approve or Reject.
+76. If approved, Yardward Pro auto-generates the QuickBooks invoice using the client's rate table
+
+    (matching load_type and weight to a rate line item).
+77. The invoice draft sits in the Invoices tab; admin reviews and pushes to QBO when ready.
+78. If rejected, you get a notification with the reason and can resubmit a corrected work order.
+4.9. End of day & clock-out
+
+               End of day form вЂ” end-of-shift tool checklist confirmation, fuel level, odometer, vehicle return location.
+
+End of day clocks you out for the day.
+79. Complete an end-of-shift tool checklist first (Forms в†’ Tool checklist).
+80. Tap End of day.
+81. Confirm the vehicle return location (yard, depot, jobsite вЂ” pre-filled).
+82. Enter the final odometer reading.
+83. Optional: fuel level (if you don't refuel and want to flag low fuel for the next driver).
+84. Optional: end-of-shift notes.
+85. Tap Submit. The form is saved; you're clocked out.
+
+    вљ пёЏ WARNING If you skip the tool checklist, the End of day form blocks submission. Yardward Pro tracks
+    tool_checklist_submissions with a kind field ('start_of_shift' vs 'end_of_shift') and refuses to clock you out
+    without the matching end-of-shift submission.
+4.10. Prepaid tickets
+
+                                    Record a prepaid ticket pull вЂ” client picker, qty entry, optional photo.
+
+Use this form when you're working a client on prepaid tickets (e.g. waste hauling). Record one ticket pull
+per load.
+86. Tap Tickets in the bottom nav.
+87. Pick the client from the dropdown.
+88. Enter the quantity of tickets pulled (usually 1).
+89. Optional: tap the camera icon to capture a photo of the physical ticket (proof for billing disputes).
+90. Tap Record. The client's balance auto-decrements; the photo (if attached) is stored in Storage.
+
+When the client's balance hits the configured threshold, admin gets a low-balance notification and
+either auto-bills a replenishment (if auto-billing is on for that client) or manually triggers one.
+4.11. Messages
+
+                                   Driver's view of Communications вЂ” thread list and conversation Sheet.
+
+Messages is the driver's view of Communications. You can:
+вЂў See every conversation you're part of
+вЂў Start a new thread with a mechanic (pick recipient, set topic, enter subject)
+вЂў Tag an admin into an existing thread when you need their input (tap the @ button in the compose
+    box)
+
+вЂў Attach photos to messages (paperclip button)
+
+Messages flow over real Twilio SMS even when you're outside the app. The mechanic gets a text on their
+phone and their reply comes back into the same thread within seconds. This is the customer-confirmed
+topology: driverв†”mechanic is the primary channel, with admin tagged when oversight is needed.
+4.12. Profile
+
+                 Profile screen вЂ” name, license info, shift status, action rows.
+
+The Profile screen shows your account details and four action rows:
+
+Field            Description
+Change password
+                 Fires a password reset email to your address. Click the
+                 link in the email and set a new password.
+Notifications   Opens a sheet with 6 toggle switches for per-user
+Help & support  notification preferences. Override the org-wide
+Logout          defaults set by admin.
+
+                Opens a sheet with FAQ accordion, mailto/tel links to
+                support, and a ticket form. Tickets go to
+                support_tickets table for admin triage.
+
+                Signs out of the app. You'll be redirected to /login.
+5. Mechanic guide
+
+The mechanic shell is a tablet/desktop sidebar layout focused on the workshop queue. Six tabs cover
+everything a mechanic does day-to-day.
+
+5.1. Workshop dashboard
+
+                        Mechanic dashboard вЂ” active MWOs assigned to me, PO submit form, low-stock alerts.
+
+The dashboard is your queue. Active maintenance work orders assigned to you are at the top, with
+vehicle ID, priority, issue summary, and the driver who reported it. Use the inline PO request form to
+submit a new parts request.
+5.2. Work orders queue
+
+                All maintenance work orders sorted by priority then creation date. Claim button for unclaimed MWOs.
+
+Maintenance work orders (MWOs) come from three sources:
+вЂў Auto-generated from flagged vehicle inspections вЂ” when a driver flags a critical defect, an MWO is
+
+    auto-created against the vehicle with priority=critical
+вЂў Driver-submitted вЂ” drivers can manually report maintenance issues via /driver/inspection's Report
+
+    issue button
+вЂў Admin-created вЂ” admin can add maintenance work directly via /admin/vehicles в†’ Add record
+Claiming an MWO
+Unclaimed MWOs in the queue have a Claim button. Tap it to assign the MWO to yourself. The
+claim_maintenance_work_order RPC uses a Postgres FOR UPDATE lock to prevent two mechanics from
+claiming the same MWO simultaneously вЂ” only one wins; the other gets an error.
+Working an MWO
+91. After claiming, the MWO moves to your active queue.
+92. Open it to see full details: vehicle, reported issue, photos from the driver, priority, source inspection
+
+    (if applicable).
+93. Update progress: add parts used, log labor hours, attach photos of the work.
+94. When finished, tap Complete. The vehicle's status moves back to operational, and last_service /
+
+    next_service_due are updated.
+95. The MWO history is preserved in maintenance_logs forever вЂ” useful for warranty claims and CVOR
+
+    audits.
+5.3. Messages
+
+    Mechanic's Communications view. Default recipient when starting a new thread is the driver from the most recent MWO.
+
+Same Communications surface as drivers, with one tweak: when you start a new conversation, the
+recipient picker defaults to the driver who reported your most recent claimed MWO. This is the most
+common case вЂ” 'I need to ask the driver who reported this fault for more details.'
+5.4. Purchase requests
+
+          Your submitted PO requests with status. Use the inline form on the dashboard or the New PO button here.
+
+Submit a PO request when you need a part that isn't in inventory. The form has:
+
+Field                                              Description
+
+Item needed                                        Free-text. As you type, Yardward Pro searches the
+                                                   parts inventory in real-time and shows matches inline.
+
+                                                   If a match exists with sufficient qty_on_hand, you're
+                                                   prompted to pull from stock instead.
+
+Quantity                                           How many of the item you need.
+
+Cost estimate                                      Your best guess at the unit cost. Helps admin approval
+
+                                                   decisions.
+
+Justification                                      Brief explanation. The maintenance work order this is
+
+                                                   tied to, or why the part is needed.
+
+On submit, the PO lands in admin's Purchase Orders tab with status='pending'. You'll get a notification
+
+when it's approved, rejected, or marked received.
+5.5. Maintenance logs
+
+                            Historical maintenance log across all vehicles. Used for compliance and warranty.
+
+Maintenance logs is the permanent record of every maintenance event across the entire fleet. Each
+entry shows:
+вЂў Vehicle, date, mechanic who did the work
+вЂў Type of maintenance (preventive, corrective, emergency)
+вЂў Description of work performed
+вЂў Parts used (with qty and cost)
+вЂў Labor hours
+вЂў Total cost
+вЂў Originating MWO (if any)
+Click any row to see full details. This data is your audit trail for CVOR compliance and warranty claims вЂ”
+never deleted, only resolved.
+5.6. Parts inventory
+
+               Parts inventory вЂ” quantity on hand, qty reserved for in-progress MWOs, reorder point.
+
+The parts inventory shows your stock levels:
+
+Field                                         Description
+
+Item name                                     Part description (e.g. 'Brake pad set вЂ” front, Isuzu
+                                              FXZ').
+
+SKU                                           Optional manufacturer or internal SKU.
+
+Qty on hand                                   Physical stock currently in the shop.
+
+Qty reserved                                  Stock allocated to in-progress MWOs but not yet
+                                              pulled. Increments when an MWO references the part.
+
+Reorder point                                 When qty_on_hand - qty_reserved drops below this,
+                                              admin gets a low-stock notification.
+
+Unit cost                                     Last known cost. Updated when POs are marked
+                                              received.
+
+Click a row to update qty_on_hand (after receiving a delivery) or edit metadata. Use the search box to
+
+find a part by name or SKU.
+6. Tokenized driver links (QR access)
+
+Tokenized driver links let you give a driver one-shot access to a specific form without them needing an
+account. Common use cases:
+
+вЂў A subcontractor driver hauling a single load for you вЂ” no need to create them an account
+вЂў A delivery driver who just needs to record a single prepaid ticket pull
+вЂў A one-time scale-house operator who needs to confirm receipt of a load
+вЂў An emergency replacement driver covering a sick employee's shift
+
+6.1. Generating a tokenized link
+
+96. Go to Settings в†’ Driver tokens.
+97. Click 'Generate token'.
+98. Pick the scope (which form the token grants access to): start_of_day, tickets, work_order,
+
+    inspection, etc.
+99. Optionally tie it to a specific driver name (for the audit log) or job ID (for context).
+100. Set the expiry (default: 24 hours).
+101. Click Generate. Yardward Pro creates a 256-bit random token via the gen_random_bytes
+
+    function and stores it in the driver_tokens table.
+102. The dialog shows you the shareable URL: /t/<token>.
+103. Click 'Copy URL' to put it on the clipboard. Send via SMS, email, or QR code.
+
+6.2. How the link works for the driver
+
+When the driver opens /t/<token> on their phone:
+
+104. The /t/$token route validates the token via the validate_driver_token RPC.
+105. If valid (not expired, not already burned), it establishes a sessionStorage-backed driver-token
+
+    session.
+106. The driver is redirected to the scoped path (e.g. /driver/tickets).
+107. They complete and submit the form вЂ” no login screen, no password.
+108. On successful submission, the token is auto-burned (status='used'); future visits to the URL get
+
+    'Token expired'.
+
+    в„№пёЏ NOTE Driver-token sessions are scope-locked. A token minted for /driver/tickets cannot be used to access
+    /driver/work-order or any other route вЂ” the route guards check the scope and bounce mismatched paths.
+7. Offline handling
+
+Drivers often work in places with poor or no cell signal вЂ” rural quarries, basement loading bays, locker
+rooms, etc. Yardward Pro handles this gracefully.
+
+7.1. How offline submission works
+
+109. Driver fills out a form (e.g. work order) and taps Submit.
+110. Yardward Pro detects there's no internet connection.
+111. Instead of failing, the submission is queued locally in IndexedDB via the offline-queue module.
+112. A small badge appears in the corner of the screen indicating N pending submissions.
+113. The driver continues working вЂ” the form is treated as submitted for all UI purposes (e.g. they
+
+    can proceed to the next step).
+114. When the device reconnects, the queue auto-flushes вЂ” every queued submission is replayed
+
+    against the API in the order it was created.
+115. On successful flush, the badge clears.
+
+7.2. Idempotency and retry safety
+
+Every queued submission carries a client-generated idempotency key. The server-side INSERT uses a
+UNIQUE constraint on (sender_id, idempotency_key) вЂ” even if the network blips and the device retries
+the same submission, the database refuses to insert a duplicate. No risk of double-submitted work
+orders or duplicate messages.
+
+7.3. Dead-letter queue
+
+If a submission fails permanently (e.g. the server rejects it due to RLS or malformed data), it lands in the
+dead-letter queue after exhausting its retry budget. Admin can review and requeue from /admin/errors
+в†’ Dead-letter tab.
+8. Notifications & alerts
+
+Yardward Pro fires notifications for every event that requires someone's attention.
+
+8.1. Notification channels
+
+вЂў In-app notifications вЂ” populate the notifications table; render in the bell badge at the top of every
+    page (click to see list)
+
+вЂў Twilio SMS вЂ” for events where the user is likely on the road (job assignments, urgent alerts)
+вЂў Email (via Resend) вЂ” for digest-style summaries (daily/weekly reports)
+
+8.2. Notification types       Description
+
+Field                         Sent to driver when admin publishes a new job
+new_job_assigned_sms          assignment.
+                              Sent to admin when driver submits a work order.
+work_order_awaiting_approval  Sent to admin + mechanic when driver flags a
+tool_flagged_on_checklist     missing/damaged tool.
+                              Sent to admin when timesheet cross-reference detects
+gps_mismatch_on_time_entry    a discrepancy.
+                              Sent to admin when mechanic submits a PO request.
+po_awaiting_approval          Sent to admin + mechanic when a vehicle exceeds its
+vehicle_maintenance_overdue   next_service_due date.
+                              Daily digest email summarizing the day's operations.
+daily_summary_email           Sent to participants when a new message lands in a
+message                       Communications thread (for inbound SMS from
+                              drivers/mechanics).
+
+8.3. Configuring preferences
+
+Org-wide defaults: Admin в†’ Settings в†’ Notifications. Per-user overrides: each user's Profile в†’
+Notifications.
+9. Integrations
+
+Five external systems are integrated. Each is configured via Supabase function secrets (set via 'supabase
+secrets set' on the operator's CLI), not via the UI.
+
+9.1. Twilio (SMS & Communications)
+
+Two distinct uses:
+
+вЂў Programmable SMS вЂ” sends one-way job-assignment notifications to drivers. Uses
+    TWILIO_ACCOUNT_SID, TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN, TWILIO_FROM_NUMBER.
+
+вЂў Conversations API вЂ” powers the Communications tab with two-way SMS threading, MMS
+    attachments, delivery receipts, and webhook-based inbound. Uses TWILIO_API_KEY_SID,
+    TWILIO_API_KEY_SECRET, TWILIO_CONVERSATIONS_SERVICE_SID, TWILIO_WEBHOOK_BASE_URL.
+
+The twilio-verify edge function checks all six credentials and the live webhook URL configuration in the
+Twilio Console. Run it any time you suspect a misconfiguration.
+
+9.2. Geotab (GPS & telematics)
+
+Geotab provides vehicle GPS, odometer, engine hours, and movement data. Used by:
+
+вЂў Live vehicle map вЂ” every 5 minutes, the geotab-sync-locations cron polls and updates
+    vehicle_locations
+
+вЂў Timesheet cross-reference вЂ” at clock-in time, the driver's GPS is compared to the vehicle's GPS at
+    the same moment
+
+вЂў Prolonged stop detection вЂ” the prolonged-stop-check cron alerts admin when a vehicle stops for >2
+    hours mid-shift
+
+вЂў Preventive maintenance scheduling вЂ” odometer thresholds trigger MWO auto-creation
+
+Configure via GEOTAB_USERNAME, GEOTAB_PASSWORD, GEOTAB_DATABASE secrets.
+
+9.3. QuickBooks Online (invoicing & payroll)
+
+Two push paths:
+
+вЂў qbo-push-invoice вЂ” when a work order is approved, generates a QBO Invoice using the client's rate
+    table for line items
+
+вЂў qbo-push-time вЂ” exports the week's approved time entries as QBO TimeActivity records (for
+    payroll)
+
+Configure via QBO_CLIENT_ID, QBO_CLIENT_SECRET, QBO_REFRESH_TOKEN, QBO_REALM_ID,
+QBO_ENVIRONMENT (sandbox or production).
+
+    вљ пёЏ WARNING Until you're ready for production billing, leave QBO_ENVIRONMENT=sandbox. Set to
+    production only after onboarding to your real QBO company.
+9.4. Fleetio (vehicle data import)
+
+One-time data migration from Fleetio. The fleetio-import edge function reads from Fleetio's API and
+bulk-imports vehicles, maintenance history, and fuel logs into the Yardward Pro tables. Configure via
+FLEETIO_BEARER_TOKEN secret. Run from /admin/vehicles в†’ Import from Fleetio.
+
+9.5. Resend (tender digest emails)
+
+Resend is the email provider for the weekly tender digest. Configure via RESEND_API_KEY,
+TENDER_DIGEST_RECIPIENTS, TENDER_DIGEST_FROM secrets. If not configured, the tender-scrape
+function still runs but skips the email send.
+
+    н ЅнІЎ TIP Resend can also be configured as Supabase's SMTP provider for password reset emails (Studio в†’ Auth
+    в†’ Settings в†’ SMTP). This gives you reliable deliverability and your own branded sender domain.
+10. Security & data isolation
+
+Yardward Pro is built with defense-in-depth security:
+
+10.1. Authentication
+
+вЂў Supabase Auth handles all authentication вЂ” JWT-based with refresh tokens
+вЂў Passwords are bcrypt-hashed at rest
+вЂў Refresh tokens rotate on every use
+вЂў Failed login attempts trigger rate limiting
+вЂў Recovery emails are scoped one-time tokens вЂ” used or expired tokens cannot be replayed
+
+10.2. Authorization via Row-Level Security
+
+Every table in Yardward Pro has RLS enabled with policies that enforce role-based isolation. Examples:
+
+Field            Description
+Drivers
+Mechanics        Can SELECT only rows where driver_id = auth.uid()
+                 Can SELECT only rows where mechanic_id = auth.uid()
+Admins           OR (role-based for shared shop resources)
+INSERT policies  Can SELECT all rows via is_admin() check
+                 WITH CHECK enforces user can only insert rows owned
+UPDATE policies  by themselves
+                 Both USING and WITH CHECK prevent re-assignment
+                 of ownership
+
+в„№пёЏ NOTE Even if a frontend bug or compromised client tried to query another user's data, Postgres would
+refuse to return the rows. RLS is enforced at the database engine level, below any application logic.
+
+10.3. Tokenized links (driver tokens)
+
+вЂў 256-bit random tokens via gen_random_bytes
+вЂў Stored hashed in the driver_tokens table (the raw token never appears in DB)
+вЂў Scope-locked вЂ” a token minted for /driver/tickets cannot access /driver/work-order
+вЂў One-shot вЂ” auto-burned on successful form submission
+вЂў Configurable expiry (default 24h)
+
+10.4. SECURITY DEFINER functions
+
+Sensitive operations (work order approval, PO approval, conversation creation, password rotation, etc.)
+run via SECURITY DEFINER Postgres functions. Each function:
+
+вЂў Has SET search_path = public, pg_temp to prevent search-path injection
+вЂў Includes an explicit role check (e.g. is_admin())
+вЂў Uses FOR UPDATE locks where atomicity matters (e.g. work order approval)
+вЂў Has REVOKE ALL FROM public, anon + GRANT EXECUTE TO authenticated, service_role
+
+10.5. Webhook signature verification
+
+Inbound webhooks (Twilio) are verified using HMAC-SHA1 signatures with constant-time byte
+comparison. Replay protection via the webhook_replay_log table prevents leaked-payload replay
+attacks. All input fields are allow-listed and regex-validated before any database write.
+11. Support & troubleshooting
+
+11.1. For drivers and mechanics
+
+Submit support tickets through Profile в†’ Help & support в†’ Open a ticket. Your admin will get the ticket
+in the support_tickets table.
+
+11.2. For admins
+
+Common issues and where to investigate:
+
+Field                                         Description
+Driver can't sign in
+Driver isn't receiving SMS                    Settings в†’ Users в†’ find the driver в†’ rotate password
+                                              via the admin-rotate-password endpoint.
+Form submission missing                       Check their phone number is real E.164 (Drivers tab в†’
+Work order not generating invoice             pencil icon). Check SMS log for delivery status. If
+                                              'failed', check Twilio Console for error code.
+Live map shows stale data                     Check Error log в†’ Dead-letter queue. May have failed
+                                              retry budget. Click Requeue to retry.
+Communications messages not delivered as SMS  Check the client's rate table has matching line items
+                                              for the work order's load_type. Check Error log for the
+                                              qbo-push-invoice function.
+                                              Click Refresh now on the map page. If still stale, check
+                                              Settings в†’ Integrations в†’ Geotab status. The geotab-
+                                              sync-locations cron might be failing.
+                                              Verify the recipient has a real E.164 phone. Check
+                                              Error log for twilio-send-message. Run twilio-verify to
+                                              confirm Conversations API configuration.
+
+11.3. For developers
+
+Yardward Pro is open-source. Issues, feature requests, and PRs welcome at https://github.com/ahsan-
+arch/yardward-pro.
+12. Glossary              Description
+
+Field                     Org-level management role with full read/write
+Admin                     access.
+CVOR                      Commercial Vehicle Operator's Registration (Ontario).
+                          Regulatory framework for commercial vehicle
+Driver token              operators.
+E.164                     Tokenized one-shot URL granting access to a specific
+Edge Function             form without signing in.
+                          International phone number format (e.g.
+MWO                       +14165550100). Required by Twilio for SMS delivery.
+Operational               Server-side serverless function deployed to Supabase.
+PWA                       Used for Twilio integration, QBO push, webhook
+PR / PO                   handlers.
+RLS                       Maintenance Work Order. Created when a vehicle
+RPC                       needs repair or scheduled maintenance.
+Service role              Vehicle status when ready for use. Other statuses:
+                          maintenance (in shop), out_of_service (parked).
+Supabase                  Progressive Web App. Installable from URL, works
+                          offline, no app store required.
+Twilio Conversations API  Purchase Request / Purchase Order. Submitted by
+                          mechanics for parts approval.
+Vercel                    Row-Level Security. Postgres feature that enforces
+WO                        row-by-row access control at the database engine.
+                          Remote Procedure Call. Postgres SECURITY DEFINER
+                          function callable from the client.
+                          Supabase API key with full database access, bypasses
+                          RLS. Used only by edge functions, never exposed to
+                          the client.
+                          The backend-as-a-service platform Yardward Pro is
+                          built on (Postgres + Auth + Realtime + Storage + Edge
+                          Functions).
+                          Twilio's multi-party threading API powering the
+                          Communications tab. Supports SMS + MMS + in-app
+                          webchat.
+                          The hosting platform for the Yardward Pro frontend.
+                          Auto-deploys on push to main.
+                          Work Order. Driver's on-site submission for a
+                          completed job. Once approved, generates an invoice.
